***manometer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:manometer.html>manometer</a> (81592)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">manomètre</i>, formed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μανός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">manós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thin, <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μέτρον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">métron</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:manometer.html>manometer</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:manometers.html>manometers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An instrument to measure pressure in a fluid, especially a double-legged liquid column gauge used to measure the difference in the pressures of two fluids.
<ul><li><b>1872</b>, <i>The American Journal of Science</i>
<dl><dd>As soon as the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:manometer.html>manometer</a></b> of the pump indicated the maximum of rarification, the apparatus <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> inclined <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1973</b>, Thomas Pynchon, <i>Gravity’s Rainbow</i>:
<dl><dd>Pökler helped in working out the Halbmodelle solution: bisecting the model lengthwise and mounting it flat-side to the wall of the test chamber, bringing the <a href = vnd.unilang:tubes.html>tubes</a> through that way to all the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:manometers.html>manometers</a></b> outside.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">manoscope</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">pressure gauge</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:manometer.html>manometer</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meetinstrument.html>meetinstrument</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarmee.html>waarmee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:druk.html>druk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemeten.html>gemeten</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a> (8369)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mantēllum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantels.html>mantels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>manteltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cape, cloak, <a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">somewhat  dated  outside certain compounds</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> coat, jacket</li>

***mantle.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a> (29209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mæntel</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mentel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sleeveless cloak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*mantil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mantilaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> reinforced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mantēllum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">covering, cloak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mantum</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">manteau</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">manto</i>), probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau">*mantos</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau">*mantalos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trodden road</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*mantos</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*mantlos</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*MenH-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tread, press together; crumble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mantles</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A piece of clothing somewhat like an open robe or cloak, especially that worn by Orthodox <a href = vnd.unilang:bishops.html>bishops</a>. <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Compare <i>mantum</i>.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from 9th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A figurative garment representing authority or status, capable of affording protection.
<dl><dd><i>At the meeting, she finally assumed the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b> of leadership of the party.</i></dd>
<dd><i>The movement strove to put women under the protective <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b> of civil rights laws.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Anything that <a href = vnd.unilang:covers.html>covers</a> or conceals something else; a cloak. <span class="defdate">[from 9th c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1599-1602</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hamlet" class="extiw" title="w:Hamlet">The Tragedy of <a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>Hamlet</a>, Prince of Denmark</a></cite>, Act 1, scene 1 |  republished as  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>Hamlet</a></cite>, New York |  Dover Publications, Inc., 1992, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 6:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But look, the <a href = vnd.unilang:morn.html>morn</a>, in russet <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b> clad, walks <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> the dew of yon high eastward hill.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1605-1606</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_Lear" class="extiw" title="w:King Lear">King Lear</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">the green <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b> of the standing pool</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">malacology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The body wall of a mollusc, from which the shell <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> secreted. <span class="defdate">[from 15th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1990</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:daniel.html>Daniel</a> L. <a href = vnd.unilang:gilbert.html>Gilbert</a>, William J. Adelman, John M. Arnold (<a href = vnd.unilang:editors.html>editors</a>), <i>Squid as Experimental Animals</i>, page 71:
<dl><dd>He grasps the female from slightly below about the mid-mantle region and positions himself so his arms are close to the opening of her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2017</b>,  Danna <a href = vnd.unilang:staaf.html>Staaf</a>,  <cite>Squid Empire</cite>, ForeEdge, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 8:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Molluscan <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a> are broadly divided into two parts: a muscular foot and a shell-secreting <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ornithology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The back of a bird together with the folded wings.</li>
<li>The zone of hot gases around a flame.</li>
<li>A gauzy fabric impregnated with metal nitrates, used in some <a href = vnd.unilang:kinds.html>kinds</a> of gas and oil lamps and lanterns, which forms a rigid but fragile mesh of metal oxides when heated during initial use and then produces white light from the heat of the flame below it. <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">So called because it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> hung above the <a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>lamp</a>'s flame like a <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a></i>.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span></li>
<li>The outer wall and casing of a blast furnace, above the hearth.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Raymond to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A penstock for a water wheel.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The cerebral cortex. <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The layer between the Earth's core and crust. <span class="defdate">[from 20th c.]</span></li>
<li>A fireplace shelf; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a></i></span></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mantling.</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">mantles</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mantling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mantled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cover or conceal (something); to cloak; to disguise.
<ul><li><b>1610-11</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tempest" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Tempest">The Tempest</a></i>, Act V, Scene I
<dl><dd>As the morning <a href = vnd.unilang:steals.html>steals</a> upon the night, Melting the darkness; so their <a href = vnd.unilang:rising.html>rising</a> senses Begin to chace the ign'rant fumes, that <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b> Their clearer reason.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1610-11</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tempest" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Tempest">The Tempest</a></i>, Act IV, Scene I
<dl><dd>I left them I' th' filthy <b>mantled</b> pool beyond your cell, There dancing up to th' chins.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To become covered or concealed. <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> add an example for this sense?)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To spread like a <a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a> (especially of blood in the face and cheeks when a person flushes).
<ul><li><b>1913</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/D.H._Lawrence" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:D.H. Lawrence">D.H. Lawrence</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sons_and_Lovers" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Sons and Lovers">Sons and <a href = vnd.unilang:lovers.html>Lovers</a></a></i>, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Sons_and_Lovers/Chapter_10" class="extiw" title="s:Sons and Lovers/Chapter 10">chapter 10</a>
<dl><dd>The blood still <b>mantled</b> below her ears; she <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> her head in shame of her humility.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***marbles.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a> (41959)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of several children's games played with small glass <a href = vnd.unilang:balls.html>balls</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Egyptian boys played <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></b> before the days of Moses.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually in a limited number of expressions</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Sanity.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">sanity</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Grandpa's <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></b>, but at least he still recognizes us.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Granny's still got all her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></b>.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">His lack of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> becoming ever more apparent.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2012</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/J._T._Petty" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:J. T. Petty">J. <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>. Petty</a>, <i>Bloody Chester</i>, First Second, →ISBN, p. 63:
<dl><dd>—Her daddy's crazy. [...] Think she's <a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>looking</a> for something? <br />—Treasure, I expect. That or maybe her daddy's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:motor.html>motor</a> racing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:bits.html>Bits</a> of rolled-up rubber shed by the tires of race cars that accumulate at the edges of the track, especially at the <a href = vnd.unilang:corners.html>corners</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:amen.html>Amen</a> Zwa,  <cite>Going Nowhere Fast In Assetto Corsa (2015-05-01)</cite>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 395:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Some <a href = vnd.unilang:corners.html>corners</a> are littered with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></b>, off the racing line.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***marginaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marginaal.html>marginaal</a> (68850)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">marginal</i>, from medieval <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">marginalis</i>, itself from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:margo.html>margo</a></i> 'edge' (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mereg-</i> "edge, boundary") + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-alis</i> '-al'
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marginaal.html>marginaal</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marginaal.html>marginaler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">marginaalst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> marginal, in or at the margin or edge(s)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> at the edge; borderline; destitute</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> socially <a href = vnd.unilang:outcast.html>outcast</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (almost) insignificant, of minor importance</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">marginaliteit</span></li></ul>

***marinier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>marinier</a> (7213)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in the mid 17th century. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>marinier</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>marinier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mariniers.html>mariniers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>mariniertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>marine</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The literal translation of "<a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>marinier</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i>marine</i>. However, a Dutch "<a href = vnd.unilang:marinier.html>marinier</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> on a par with a US Navy SEAL. A US Marine <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> somewhat equivalent to a Dutch Landmacht <a href = vnd.unilang:soldaat.html>soldaat</a>.</li></ul>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:beroep.html>beroep</a>)</span> <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:militair.html>militair</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:militaire.html>militaire</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eenheid.html>eenheid</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderdeel.html>onderdeel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> marine, <a href = vnd.unilang:bestaande.html>bestaande</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> getrainde, gespecialiseerde <a href = vnd.unilang:infanteristen.html>infanteristen</a>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">market</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">marct</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*markat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">marcātus</i>, an alternative form of Classical <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mercātus</i>.
</p>

***marlin.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marlin.html>marlin</a> (16516)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">marlinspike</i>, named so because of its pointed snout.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:marlin.html>marlin</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:marlin.html>marlin</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">marlins</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any species of game fish belonging to either of the genera <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Tetrapturus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Tetrapturus"><i>Tetrapturus</i></a></span> or <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Makaira" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Makaira"><i>Makaira</i></a></span>. Every such species <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a pointed, spear-like projection of the upper jaw.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">spearfish</span></li></ul>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:marmelade.html>marmelade</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jam, preserve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a> (60134)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">marron</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">feral; fugitive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">adjective</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">cimarrón</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fugitive, wild, feral</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ta%C3%ADno_language" class="extiw" title="w:Taíno language">Taíno</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maroon_(people)" class="extiw" title="w:Maroon (people)"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>Maroon</a> (people)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maroon_(people)" class="extiw" title="w:Maroon (people)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">maroons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An escaped negro slave of the Caribbean and the Americas or a descendant of escaped slaves. <span class="defdate">[from 17th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1985</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wade_Davis_(anthropologist)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wade Davis (anthropologist)"><a href = vnd.unilang:wade.html>Wade</a> Davis</a>, <i>The Serpent and the Rainbow</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> amp; Schuster, p. 193:
<dl><dd>Further north a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>Maroon</a></b> community in the Bahoruco Mountains thrived for eighty-five years, until the French proposed a truce under the <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> of which the <b>Maroons</b> would be permitted to form an independent clan.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2007</b>, Kevin Filan, <i>The Haitian Vodou Handbook</i>, Destiny Books 2007, p. 14:
<dl><dd>Joining others who <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> escaped before them, they formed communities of <b>Maroons</b> in which many traditional African customs and social mores <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> preserved.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A castaway; a person who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> marooned. <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">castaway</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Associated with <a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>Maroon</a> culture, communities or peoples.
<ul><li><b>2002</b>, Cynthia James, <i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>Maroon</a> Narrative: Caribbean Literature in English Across Boundaries, Ethnicities, and Centuries</i>, Heinemann Educational Books
<dl><dd>In her discussion of Michelle <a href = vnd.unilang:cliff.html>Cliff</a>'s <i>Abeng</i>, a novel that historicizes <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> culture and the Jamaican warrior heroine Nanny of the Maroons, Francoise Lionnet examines linguistic “metissage” <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">maroons</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">marooning</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">marooned</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To abandon in a remote, desolate place, as on a desert island.
<ul><li><b>2010</b>, Brogan Steele, <i>From the <a href = vnd.unilang:jaws.html>Jaws</a> of Death: Extreme True Adventures of <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vs.html>vs</a>. Nature</i>, St. Martin's <a href = vnd.unilang:griffin.html>Griffin</a> (→ISBN), page <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.de/books?id=pRQsO5OVLTcCamp;lpg=PA231amp;dq=%22marooned%22amp;hl=deamp;pg=PA231v=onepage">231</a>:
<dl><dd>After the harrowing <a href = vnd.unilang:stories.html>stories</a> of being <b>marooned</b> at sea and stranded in the frozen wastelands of Alaska and the <a href = vnd.unilang:poles.html>Poles</a>, one would think that survival on dry <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> would be easier <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">marron</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chestnut; brown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">marrone</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chestnut; brown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μάραον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">máraon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sweet chestnut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare Spanish <span class="Latn" lang="es">marrón</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maroon_(color)" class="extiw" title="w:Maroon (color)"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>Maroon</a> (color)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maroon_(color)" class="extiw" title="w:Maroon (color)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">maroons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A rich dark red, somewhat brownish, color.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a> colour: <span style="background-color:800000; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2009</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>Ben</a> Long, <i>The Nikon D90 Companion: Practical Photography Advice You Can Take Anywhere</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>'Reilly Media, Inc. (→ISBN), page <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.de/books?id=3ukYp2HE9KQCamp;lpg=PA176amp;dq=%22a%20maroon%22amp;hl=deamp;pg=PA176v=onepage">176</a>:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> it a really dark <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> or a lighter <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> or a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> that leans toward the red side? Or the <a href = vnd.unilang:magenta.html>magenta</a> side? To address this issue, scientists use something called a color space.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> color</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown. Possibly owing to the fact that the color of a fired flare <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> commonly red.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/maroon_(rocket)" class="extiw" title="w:maroon (rocket)"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a> (rocket)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/maroon_(rocket)" class="extiw" title="w:maroon (rocket)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">maroons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A rocket-propelled firework or skyrocket, often one used as a signal (e.g. to summon the crew of a lifeboat or warn of an air raid).
<ul><li><b>1887</b>, “Metropolitan Reports,” <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chemist_%2B_Druggist" class="extiw" title="w:Chemist + Druggist">The Chemist and Druggist</a></i>, 5 November, 1887, p. 564,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/b19974760M0437">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>On Sunday afternoon a serious firework explosion occurred in Lambeth, whereby three persons <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> seriously injured. Two lads <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> purchased a firework called a “<b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b>”, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a bomb consisting of a small ball of string covered with a red composition. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> loaded with gunpowder, and there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also a fuse attached.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1891</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Archer_(critic)" class="extiw" title="w:William Archer (critic)">William <a href = vnd.unilang:archer.html>Archer</a></a> (translator), “At the Fair” in <i>Tales of Two Countries</i> by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Kielland" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alexander Kielland">Alexander Kielland</a>, New York: Harper, p. 73,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/talesoftwocountr00kieliala">[2]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>As the evening falls, colored lamps and Chinese lanterns are lighted around the venerable oak which <a href = vnd.unilang:stands.html>stands</a> in the middle of the fairground and boys climb about among its topmost <a href = vnd.unilang:branches.html>branches</a> with <b>maroons</b> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bengal_light" class="extiw" title="w:Bengal light">Bengal lights</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1900</b>, Alan C. Jenkins, <i>Introducing <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>Horses</a></i>, London: Spring Books,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/introducinghorse00jenk">[3]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Many a seaman’s life may have depended on equine speed and strength. Some of these ‘Lifeboat <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>Horses</a>’ used to recognise the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> fired to summon the Lifeboat crew. Long after its retirement one of the <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a> which regularly helped to haul the Hoylake Lifeboat <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b> fired one day when it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> working in the neighbouring fields. It immediately became very excited and made for the boathouse.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1932</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_Bernard_Shaw" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:George Bernard Shaw">George <a href = vnd.unilang:bernard.html>Bernard</a> Shaw</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Too_True_to_Be_Good" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Too True to Be Good">Too True to Be Good</a></i>, Act II,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://gutenberg.net.au/ebooks03/0300591h.html">[4]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>And now I am off to inspect stores. There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a shortage of <b>maroons</b> that I don’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> understand.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1933</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/H._G._Wells" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:H. G. Wells">H. G. Wells</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Shape_of_Things_to_Come" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Shape of Things to Come">The Shape of <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>Things</a> to Come</a></i>, Book 2, Chapter 9,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.net.au/ebooks03/0301391h.html">[5]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>The big air <a href = vnd.unilang:raids.html>raids</a> <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> much more dreadful than the air <a href = vnd.unilang:raids.html>raids</a> of the World War. They began with a nightmare of warning <b>maroons</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sirens.html>sirens</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hooters.html>hooters</a> and the shrill whistles of cyclist <a href = vnd.unilang:scouts.html>scouts</a>, then swarms of frantic people running to and fro <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From an intentional mispronunciation of the word <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">moron</i> used by the cartoon character <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bugs_Bunny" class="extiw" title="w:Bugs Bunny"><a href = vnd.unilang:bugs.html>Bugs</a> Bunny</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">maroons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An idiot; a fool.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">fool</span>, Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">idiot</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2011</b>, S. Watts <a href = vnd.unilang:taylor.html>Taylor</a>, <i>Tarnish</i>, IUniverse (2011), →ISBN, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=jqn8HMZTeRICamp;pg=PA21">page 21</a>:
<dl><dd>At least, I would not be sleeping that night. Why <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> I have that espresso? What a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maroon.html>maroon</a></b>!</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***marr.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marr.html>marr</a> (46955)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*marhaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mearh</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">mar</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">marah</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌼𐌰𐍂𐌷𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">marhs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="non"><a href = vnd.unilang:marr.html>marr</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>horse</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:mari.html>mari</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*móri</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>mere</a></i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>mere</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>mere</a></i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">mar</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">meri</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>Meer</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">meri</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>Meer</a></i>).
</p>
